<p data-start="157" data-end="179"><strong data-start="157" data-end="179">1. Share your code</strong></p>

<p data-start="276" data-end="324"><strong data-start="276" data-end="314">2. Tell me what you want to change</strong><br>
Examples:</p>

<li data-section-id="i7mjwz" data-start="325" data-end="367">

</li>
</ul>

data-start="14" data-end="59">yes—but not directly from pure HTML alone</strong>, especially on GitHub Pages. You’ll need a small workaround depending on how automated you want this to be.</p>
<p data-start="169" data-end="234">Let me break it down clearly so you can choose the best approach.</p>
<hr data-start="236" data-end="239">
<h1 data-section-id="lp5fno" data-start="241" data-end="276">⚠️ The important limitation first</h1>
<p data-start="277" data-end="398">Platforms like <strong data-start="292" data-end="333"><span class="hover:entity-accent entity-underline inline cursor-pointer align-baseline"><span class="whitespace-normal">eBay</span></span></strong> don’t allow simple “scrape it from HTML” in a clean way because:</p>
<ul data-start="399" data-end="510">
<li data-section-id="1juzo6t" data-start="399" data-end="443">
<p data-start="401" data-end="443">Their pages are dynamic (JavaScript-heavy)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1j2no7b" data-start="444" data-end="468">
<p data-start="446" data-end="468">They restrict scraping</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1emj3zf" data-start="469" data-end="510">
<p data-start="471" data-end="510">GitHub Pages is <strong data-start="487" data-end="497">static</strong> (no backend)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="512" data-end="534">So you can’t just say:</p>
<blockquote data-start="535" data-end="588">
<p data-start="537" data-end="588">“Pull all my eBay products automatically into HTML”</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-start="590" data-end="635">…but you <em data-start="599" data-end="604">can</em> still do this in smart ways 👇</p>
<hr data-start="637" data-end="640">
<h1 data-section-id="sz49fy" data-start="642" data-end="683">✅ Option 1 — Manual (Simple &amp; reliable)</h1>
<p data-start="684" data-end="728">Best if you want something quick and stable.</p>
<h3 data-section-id="174qew3" data-start="730" data-end="747">How it works:</h3>
<ul data-start="748" data-end="858">
<li data-section-id="13g8bjr" data-start="748" data-end="816">
<p data-start="750" data-end="777">Copy product info manually:</p>
<ul data-start="780" data-end="816">
<li data-section-id="177vps8" data-start="780" data-end="787">
<p data-start="782" data-end="787">Title</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="174vkzp" data-start="790" data-end="797">
<p data-start="792" data-end="797">Price</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="16t8r8v" data-start="800" data-end="807">
<p data-start="802" data-end="807">Image</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1j3unns" data-start="810" data-end="816">
<p data-start="812" data-end="816">Link</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1614b6c" data-start="817" data-end="858">
<p data-start="819" data-end="858">Paste into your HTML as “product cards”</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="147dq04" data-start="860" data-end="892">Why this works well for you:</h3>
<ul data-start="893" data-end="1006">
<li data-section-id="9nk15t" data-start="893" data-end="948">
<p data-start="895" data-end="948">You said it's just a <strong data-start="916" data-end="948">reference page for a chatbot</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="51dm4c" data-start="949" data-end="981">
<p data-start="951" data-end="981">Doesn’t need real-time updates</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1len8kl" data-start="982" data-end="1006">
<p data-start="984" data-end="1006">Super easy to maintain</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1008" data-end="1078">👉 I can convert your template into a <strong data-start="1046" data-end="1068">clean product grid</strong> for this.</p>
<hr data-start="1080" data-end="1083">
<h1 data-section-id="7o13ps" data-start="1085" data-end="1130">⚙️ Option 2 — Semi-automatic (Best balance)</h1>
<p data-start="1131" data-end="1187">Use a script to extract data, then paste into your site.</p>
<h3 data-section-id="wsiwnb" data-start="1189" data-end="1210">Example workflow:</h3>
<ol data-start="1211" data-end="1326">
<li data-section-id="4kg2t0" data-start="1211" data-end="1271">
<p data-start="1214" data-end="1218">Use:</p>
<ul data-start="1222" data-end="1271">
<li data-section-id="1ey8n7y" data-start="1222" data-end="1240">
<p data-start="1224" data-end="1240">Python script OR</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1umcn5l" data-start="1244" data-end="1271">
<p data-start="1246" data-end="1271">Browser extension scraper</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-section-id="11f03y0" data-start="1272" data-end="1302">
<p data-start="1275" data-end="1285">Export to:</p>
<ul data-start="1289" data-end="1302">
<li data-section-id="3fvgaz" data-start="1289" data-end="1302">
<p data-start="1291" data-end="1302">JSON or CSV</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-section-id="l0jriz" data-start="1303" data-end="1326">
<p data-start="1306" data-end="1326">Paste into your HTML</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="1328" data-end="1345">Tools people use:</p>
<ul data-start="1346" data-end="1453">
<li data-section-id="lyf7sl" data-start="1346" data-end="1385">
<p data-start="1348" data-end="1385"><span class="hover:entity-accent entity-underline inline cursor-pointer align-baseline"><span class="whitespace-normal">ParseHub</span></span></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="wlg39x" data-start="1386" data-end="1425">
<p data-start="1388" data-end="1425"><span class="hover:entity-accent entity-underline inline cursor-pointer align-baseline"><span class="whitespace-normal">Octoparse</span></span></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="xybdup" data-start="1426" data-end="1453">
<p data-start="1428" data-end="1453">Or a simple Python script</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1455" data-end="1512">👉 This is probably the <strong data-start="1479" data-end="1512">best option for your use case</strong></p>
<hr data-start="1514" data-end="1517">
<h1 data-section-id="1j2ikix" data-start="1519" data-end="1561">🔌 Option 3 — eBay API (Fully automated)</h1>
<p data-start="1562" data-end="1592">Most powerful, but more setup.</p>
<p data-start="1594" data-end="1598">Use:</p>
<ul data-start="1599" data-end="1638">
<li data-section-id="1etlrsl" data-start="1599" data-end="1638">
<p data-start="1601" data-end="1638"><span class="hover:entity-accent entity-underline inline cursor-pointer align-baseline"><span class="whitespace-normal">eBay Developer APIs</span></span></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="eqnika" data-start="1640" data-end="1654">You would:</h3>
<ul data-start="1655" data-end="1713">
<li data-section-id="1dw2exd" data-start="1655" data-end="1668">
<p data-start="1657" data-end="1668">Get API key</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="myfrtx" data-start="1669" data-end="1685">
<p data-start="1671" data-end="1685">Fetch listings</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="j7dn6z" data-start="1686" data-end="1713">
<p data-start="1688" data-end="1713">Load them with JavaScript</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="1x8jovr" data-start="1715" data-end="1727">Problem:</h3>
<ul data-start="1728" data-end="1823">
<li data-section-id="19klqv3" data-start="1728" data-end="1783">
<p data-start="1730" data-end="1783">GitHub Pages = no backend → harder to secure API keys</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1sxs1ut" data-start="1784" data-end="1823">
<p data-start="1786" data-end="1823">Overkill for a simple chatbot dataset</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1825" data-end="1828">
<h1 data-section-id="1iwf1pq" data-start="1830" data-end="1874">🧠 What I recommend (for YOU specifically)</h1>
<p data-start="1875" data-end="1891">Given your goal:</p>
<blockquote data-start="1892" data-end="1931">
<p data-start="1894" data-end="1931">“Reference page for chatbot learning”</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-start="1933" data-end="1946">Go with this:</p>
<h3 data-section-id="1st95ef" data-start="1948" data-end="1982">✔️ Structured static data page</h3>
<ul data-start="1983" data-end="2055">
<li data-section-id="2n5tv2" data-start="1983" data-end="2013">
<p data-start="1985" data-end="2013">Build a <strong data-start="1993" data-end="2013">Products section</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="18rc5dj" data-start="2014" data-end="2055">
<p data-start="2016" data-end="2055">Each item = clean structured HTML like:</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h1 data-section-id="9tgd4p" data-start="164" data-end="208"><span role="text">🧠 First: what you <em data-start="185" data-end="190">can</em> extract from eBay</span></h1>
<p data-start="209" data-end="280">Each listing (like your product link) contains structured info such as:</p>
<ul data-start="281" data-end="380">
<li data-section-id="16xunuw" data-start="281" data-end="290">
<p data-start="283" data-end="290">Title</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="n3xp8l" data-start="291" data-end="300">
<p data-start="293" data-end="300">Price</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="gmtinw" data-start="301" data-end="311">
<p data-start="303" data-end="311">Images</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ou33i3" data-start="312" data-end="325">
<p data-start="314" data-end="325">Condition</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1s4k63x" data-start="326" data-end="364">
<p data-start="328" data-end="364">Item specifics (brand, size, etc.)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1c9tvn2" data-start="365" data-end="380">
<p data-start="367" data-end="380">Description</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="382" data-end="491">eBay itself even generates a short summary from this data automatically <span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center select-none relative top-[-0.094rem] animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]" data-testid="webpage-citation-pill" style="width: 37px;"><a href="https://pages.ebay.com/mc/en-us/sellerinformation/news/sprupd16/view-item.html?utm_source=chatgpt.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://pages.ebay.com/mc/en-us/sellerinformation/news/sprupd16/view-item.html?utm_source=chatgpt.com" class="flex h-4.5 overflow-hidden rounded-xl px-2 text-[9px] font-medium transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! select-none" style="max-width: 37px;"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="max-w-[15ch] grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">eBay</span></span></span></a></span></span></p>
<p data-start="493" data-end="526">👉 So yes, the data is there—but…</p>
<hr data-start="528" data-end="531">
<h1 data-section-id="181vcx7" data-start="533" data-end="565">⚠️ The key problem (important)</h1>
<p data-start="566" data-end="642">You <strong data-start="570" data-end="633">cannot reliably “pull” that data directly into GitHub Pages</strong> because:</p>
<ul data-start="643" data-end="745">
<li data-section-id="eoa2k7" data-start="643" data-end="678">
<p data-start="645" data-end="678">eBay blocks most scraping methods</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1prm3tj" data-start="679" data-end="717">
<p data-start="681" data-end="717">Pages are dynamic (JavaScript-heavy)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="15xky0l" data-start="718" data-end="745">
<p data-start="720" data-end="745">GitHub Pages = no backend</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="747" data-end="769">So this will NOT work:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="770" data-end="847"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full <hr data-start="849" data-end="852">
<h1 data-section-id="13o1q4z" data-start="854" data-end="906">✅ Best solution for YOUR setup (simple + powerful)</h1>
<h2 data-section-id="1jt2u5x" data-start="908" data-end="966">🔧 Option I recommend: “Extract once → store → display”</h2>
<h3 data-section-id="1ijchkm" data-start="968" data-end="1014">Step 1 — Extract the data (semi-automatic)</h3>
<p data-start="1015" data-end="1032">Use one of these:</p>
<ul data-start="1033" data-end="1123">
<li data-section-id="rkgfy1" data-start="1033" data-end="1062">
<p data-start="1035" data-end="1062">Browser extension scraper</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1bj5gvg" data-start="1063" data-end="1086">
<p data-start="1065" data-end="1086">Small Python script</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="199nai0" data-start="1087" data-end="1123">
<p data-start="1089" data-end="1123">Manual copy (totally fine for now)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1125" data-end="1154">From your product page, grab:</p>
<ul data-start="1155" data-end="1235">
<li data-section-id="177vps8" data-start="1155" data-end="1162">
<p data-start="1157" data-end="1162">Title</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="174vkzp" data-start="1163" data-end="1170">
<p data-start="1165" data-end="1170">Price</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1fqcfr8" data-start="1171" data-end="1182">
<p data-start="1173" data-end="1182">Image URL</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="b403uj" data-start="1183" data-end="1194">
<p data-start="1185" data-end="1194">Condition</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1cx113y" data-start="1195" data-end="1228">
<p data-start="1197" data-end="1228">Key details (size, brand, etc.)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1j3unns" data-start="1229" data-end="1235">
<p data-start="1231" data-end="1235">Link</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1237" data-end="1240">
<h3 data-section-id="9jhfwx" data-start="1242" data-end="1298">Step 2 — Store it in JSON (this is the game changer)</h3>
<p data-start="1299" data-end="1342">Instead of raw HTML, create something like:</p>

<p data-start="1697" data-end="1733">👉 This is PERFECT for your chatbot:</p>
<ul data-start="1734" data-end="1770">
<li data-section-id="16xd4y5" data-start="1734" data-end="1741">
<p data-start="1736" data-end="1741">Clean</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1w6jkt5" data-start="1742" data-end="1754">
<p data-start="1744" data-end="1754">Structured</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1b3u44o" data-start="1755" data-end="1770">
<p data-start="1757" data-end="1770">Easy to parse</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1772" data-end="1775">
<h3 data-section-id="t410bz" data-start="1777" data-end="1812">Step 3 — Render it in your HTML</h3>
<p data-start="1813" data-end="1847">Then use JavaScript to display it:</p>

<hr data-start="2298" data-end="2301">
<h1 data-section-id="s1d9mk" data-start="2303" data-end="2342">🤖 Why this is ideal for your chatbot</h1>
<p data-start="2343" data-end="2364">This setup gives you:</p>
<ul data-start="2365" data-end="2465">
<li data-section-id="wkvcx2" data-start="2365" data-end="2408">
<p data-start="2367" data-end="2408">Structured dataset (like a mini database)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="d626dx" data-start="2409" data-end="2431">
<p data-start="2411" data-end="2431">Easy to expand later</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="wb7q06" data-start="2432" data-end="2465">
<p data-start="2434" data-end="2465">Works perfectly with AI parsing</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="2467" data-end="2505">👉 Way better than scraping live pages</p>

<h1 data-section-id="1iw2zpe" data-start="3611" data-end="3648">🧠 How you’ll use it (super simple)</h1>
<p data-start="3650" data-end="3667">For each product:</p>
<ul data-start="3668" data-end="3803">
<li data-section-id="15ep71s" data-start="3668" data-end="3692">
<p data-start="3670" data-end="3692">Open your eBay listing</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="dp95xv" data-start="3693" data-end="3803">
<p data-start="3695" data-end="3700">Copy:</p>
<ul data-start="3703" data-end="3803">
<li data-section-id="177vps8" data-start="3703" data-end="3710">
<p data-start="3705" data-end="3710">Title</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="174vkzp" data-start="3713" data-end="3720">
<p data-start="3715" data-end="3720">Price</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="18p0zjf" data-start="3723" data-end="3765">
<p data-start="3725" data-end="3765">Image (right-click → copy image address)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1j3unns" data-start="3768" data-end="3774">
<p data-start="3770" data-end="3774">Link</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="twsk11" data-start="3777" data-end="3803">
<p data-start="3779" data-end="3803">Size / brand / condition</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="3805" data-end="3818">Then replace:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="3819" data-end="3870"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"><div class="border border-token-border-light border-radius-3xl corner-superellipse/1.1 rounded-3xl"><div class="h-full w-full border-radius-3xl bg-token-bg-elevated-secondary corner-superellipse/1.1 overflow-clip rounded-3xl lxnfua_clipPathFallback"><div class="pointer-events-none absolute end-1.5 top-1 z-2 md:end-2 md:top-1"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none pointer-events-auto py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-black/5 dark:hover:bg-white/10 size-9 rounded-full px-2" aria-label="Copy" data-state="closed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-md"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-97566a9e.svg#ce3544" fill="currentColor"></use></svg></button></div><div class="relative"><div class="pe-11 pt-3" style="transform: none;"><div class="relative z-0 flex max-w-full"><div id="code-block-viewer" dir="ltr" class="q9tKkq_viewer cm-editor z-10 light:cm-light dark:cm-light flex h-full w-full flex-col items-stretch ͼ5 ͼj"><div class="cm-scroller"><div class="cm-content q9tKkq_readonly"><span>IMAGE_URL_1</span><br><span>Product Title 1</span><br><span>$XX</span><br><span>EBAY_LINK_1</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class=""><div class="" style="width: 100%; transform: none;"></div></div></div></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="3872" data-end="3875">
<h1 data-section-id="18fdbz5" data-start="3877" data-end="3916">🤖 Bonus (important for your chatbot)</h1>
<p data-start="3917" data-end="3959">Because your data is clean and consistent:</p>
<ul data-start="3960" data-end="4062">
<li data-section-id="12vcdcw" data-start="3960" data-end="4001">
<p data-start="3962" data-end="4001">Your chatbot can easily “read” the page</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="hsna60" data-start="4002" data-end="4062">
<p data-start="4004" data-end="4062">You can later upgrade to JSON without rewriting everything</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="4064" data-end="4067">
<h1 data-section-id="1b7tb21" data-start="4069" data-end="4122">🔥 Optional upgrade (tell me if you want this next)</h1>
<p data-start="4123" data-end="4134">I can also:</p>
<ul data-start="4135" data-end="4326">
<li data-section-id="15a85x" data-start="4135" data-end="4174">

<hr data-start="2292" data-end="2295">
<h1 data-section-id="vg4auw" data-start="2297" data-end="2353">⚠️ Important note (so you don’t run into issues later)</h1>
<p data-start="2355" data-end="2408">Those image URLs (<code data-start="2373" data-end="2388">i.ebayimg.com</code>) usually work, but:</p>
<ul data-start="2409" data-end="2492">
<li data-section-id="btyb1d" data-start="2409" data-end="2449">
<p data-start="2411" data-end="2449">They can change or expire occasionally</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1u5kdbd" data-start="2450" data-end="2492">
<p data-start="2452" data-end="2492">eBay doesn’t guarantee permanent hosting</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="2494" data-end="2532">👉 Best practice (optional but solid):</p>
<ul data-start="2533" data-end="2608">
<li data-section-id="1g0cifc" data-start="2533" data-end="2550">
<p data-start="2535" data-end="2550">Download images</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="uvzv1" data-start="2551" data-end="2597">
<p data-start="2553" data-end="2597">Upload them to your GitHub repo (<code data-start="2586" data-end="2596">/images/</code>)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="iw8cwu" data-start="2598" data-end="2608">
<p data-start="2600" data-end="2608">Replace:</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h1 data-section-id="35z5ax" data-start="2607" data-end="2631">🧠 What this gives you</h1>
<p data-start="2633" data-end="2651">Now your site can:</p>
<ul data-start="2652" data-end="2803">
<li data-section-id="1lmu7y9" data-start="2652" data-end="2729">
<p data-start="2654" data-end="2667">🔍 Search by:</p>
<ul data-start="2670" data-end="2729">
<li data-section-id="177vps8" data-start="2670" data-end="2677">
<p data-start="2672" data-end="2677">Title</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="16ybzhv" data-start="2680" data-end="2687">
<p data-start="2682" data-end="2687">Brand</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1j4dcvh" data-start="2690" data-end="2696">
<p data-start="2692" data-end="2696">Size</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="8tviw0" data-start="2699" data-end="2729">
<p data-start="2701" data-end="2729">Any text inside product card</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li data-section-id="h6ecjn" data-start="2730" data-end="2763">
<p data-start="2732" data-end="2763">⚡ Instant filtering (no reload)</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1hud4nw" data-start="2764" data-end="2803">
<p data-start="2766" data-end="2803">💻 Works on GitHub Pages (no backend)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="2805" data-end="2808">
<h1 data-section-id="eogvgk" data-start="2810" data-end="2838">⚠️ Small but important fix</h1>
<p data-start="2840" data-end="2884">Make sure ALL your products have this class:</p>
<pre class="overflow-visible! px-0!" data-start="2886" data-end="2910"><div class="relative w-full mt-4 mb-1"><div class=""><div class="relative"><div class="h-full min-h-0 min-w-0"><div class="h-full justify-self-start text-token-text-primary"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="icon-sm me-2.5 shrink-0"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-97566a9e.svg#e45ab3" fill="currentColor"></use></svg>HTML</div><div class="flex flex-row items-center gap-0.5 justify-self-end"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center BRAUNBÄR

We are proud to launch our shop with this iconic historical piece. We meticulously source only the finest vintage denim to ensure our customers receive authentic, high-quality garments that tell a story.

Vintage Levi's 501XX – Valencia St. Factory (1995)

This is a true collector's gem: an original pair of Levi's 501-0000 manufactured in October 1995 at the legendary Valencia Street plant in San Francisco. Highly sought after for its superior construction and historical significance, identified by the "555" stamp on the back of the top button and internal care tag.

The Valencia St. factory is world-renowned for its superior construction and historical significance, using the highest quality denim produced before the closure of Levi's original U.S. plants.

HEM &amp; LENGTH DETAILS:
Note: While the original tag says L32, these have been professionally hemmed to a 29.5-inch actual inseam. Please check measurements carefully to ensure a perfect fit.

ITEM SPECIFICS
• Model: 501-0000 (Button Fly)
• Factory Code: 555 (Valencia St., San Francisco)
• Production Date: 10/1995
• Origin: Made in USA
• Condition: Excellent Vintage Condition

CONDITION DETAILS
This pair features a beautiful Natural Indigo Fade with authentic vintage character. The denim remains heavy, stiff, and durable— features authentic “train track” fading along the seams and subtle factory weaving slubs — characteristic of the high-quality 90s 501XX production. All original rivets and buttons are intact.

MEASUREMENTS (Lying Flat)
• Waist: 34"
• Inseam: 29.5"
• Rise: Mid (10–12")
• Leg Opening: 8"

Please refer to actual measurements rather than tag size, as vintage garments may vary over time.

SHIPPING &amp; SERVICE
We ship quickly and with care. Each garment is securely packaged to ensure it arrives as described. International buyers are welcome via eBay International Shipping. We ship within 1-2 business days with tracking provided.

Ref: 021-A
